      "#Transformer Design for a HVDC Transmission System\n",
      "The purpose of this project is to design AC / AC transformer for using in HVDC transmission line.\n",
      "\n",
      "Specifications of Transformer\n",
      "\n",
      "*6.5 MVA*,Single Phase transformer,\n",
      "\n",
      "*Operating Frequency: 500 Hz\n",
      "\n",
      "*Input Voltage: 3 kV\n",
      "\n",
      "*Output Voltage: 300kV\n",
      "\n",
      "*Operating Temperature 110 \u00b0C"
     ]
    },

      "3) Selection of Proper Cables\n",
      "\n",
      "4) Determination of Other Core Dimensions\n",
      "\n",
      "5) Copper and Core Loss Calculations\n",
      "\n",
      "6) Efficiency Calculations\n",
      "\n",

      "\n",
      "8) Vout Calculations at Full Load\n",

      "9) Results\n",
      "\n",
      "10) Conclusion and Comments"

     "metadata": {},
     "source": [
      "**1)CORE SELECTION AND CORE LOSS CALCULATION**"
     ]
    },
    {
     "cell_type": "markdown",
     "metadata": {},
     "source": [
      "**A) Core-Material-1**"
     ]
    },
    {
     "cell_type": "code",
     "collapsed": false,
     "input": [
      "#Electrical Steel,  Grade EN10106, M235-35A, 0.35 mm thickness\n",
      "\n",
      "B1=1.5 # T max\n",
      "density1=7.6 # g/cm3\n",
      "\n",
      "#In order to calculate Core loss at 500 Hz , Steinmetz equation is used\n",
      "#Steinmetz equation, Pcore=k*(f^a)*(B^b)\n",
      "#From datasheet of core\n",
      "#We need to find \"a\" in steinmetz equaion by using linearity\n",
      "Pcore_loss_50_material1=2.35 # W/kg at 50Hz at 1.5 T \n",
      "PCore_loss_400_material1=41.9 # W/kg at 400Hz at 1.5 T\n",
      "a=log(PCore_loss_400_material1/ Pcore_loss_50_material1)/log(400.0/50.0)\n",
      "Pcore_loss_500_material1=(500.0/400.0)**a*PCore_loss_400_material1\n",
      "print 'Pcoreloss at 500 Hz for material-1=',Pcore_loss_500_material1,'W/kg'\n"
     ],
     "language": "python",
     "metadata": {},
     "outputs": [
      {
       "output_type": "stream",
       "stream": "stdout",
       "text": [
        "Pcoreloss at 500 Hz for material-1= 57.07865396 W/kg\n"
       ]
      }
     ],
     "prompt_number": 13
    },
    {
     "cell_type": "markdown",
     "metadata": {},
     "source": [
      "[Core DataSheet ,Grade EN10106, M25-35A](http://perso.uclouvain.be/ernest.matagne/ELEC2311/T2006/NOFP.pdf)"
     ]
    },
    {
     "cell_type": "markdown",
     "metadata": {},
     "source": [
      "**B) Core-Material-2**"
     ]
    },
    {
     "cell_type": "code",
     "collapsed": false,
     "input": [
      "#ATI Grain Oriented Electrical Steel M-2\n",
      "\n",
      "B2=1.5 # T max\n",
      "density2=7.65 # g/cm3\n",
      "\n",
      "#In order to calculate Core loss at 500 Hz , Steinmetz equation is used\n",
      "#Steinmetz equation, Pcore=k*(f^a)*(B^b)\n",
      "#From datasheet of core\n",
      "#We need to find \"a\" in steinmetz equaion by using linearity\n",
      "Pcore_loss_50_material2=0.668 # W/kg at 50Hz at 1.5 T \n",
      "PCore_loss_60_material2=0.9 # W/kg at 400Hz at 1.5 T\n",
      "a=log(PCore_loss_60_material2/ Pcore_loss_50_material2)/log(60.0/50.0)\n",
      "Pcore_loss_500_material2=(500.0/60.0)**a*PCore_loss_60_material2\n",
      "print 'Pcoreloss at 500 Hz for material-2=',Pcore_loss_500_material2,'W/kg'\n"
     ],
     "language": "python",
     "metadata": {},
     "outputs": [
      {
       "output_type": "stream",
       "stream": "stdout",
       "text": [
        "Pcoreloss at 500 Hz for material-2= 28.8294224543 W/kg\n"
       ]
      }
     ],
     "prompt_number": 14

    {
     "cell_type": "markdown",
     "metadata": {},
     "source": [
      "[Core DataSheet ,ATI Grain Oriented Electrical Steel M-2](https://www.atimetals.com/Documents/goes_technical_data2_v1.pdf)"
     ]

     "cell_type": "heading",

     "metadata": {},
     "source": [
      "**2)TURN NUMBER AND CORE AREA DETERMANITION**"
     ]
    },
    {
     "cell_type": "code",
     "collapsed": false,
     "input": [
      "K_lamination=0.96 # Stacking Factor\n",
      "E1=3000.0 \n",
      "# E1=4.44*N1*Ac*f*B*K_laminitation\n",
      "# Let'S find N1 X A\n",
      "N1Ac=E1/(4.44*500.0*1.5*0.96)\n",
      "print'N1xAc=',N1Ac\n",
      "#Let's say primary winding turn number:18\n",
      "N1=18\n",
      "N2=N1*100 \n",
      "Ac=N1Ac/N1\n",
      "# square core dimension calculation ,x\n",
      "x=sqrt(Ac*1000000)\n",
      "print 'N1=',N1,'turns'\n",
      "print 'N2=',N2,'turns'\n",
      "print 'x=',x,'mm'\n",
      "I2=6.5*10**6 / 300000.0\n",
      "print 'I2=',I2,'A'\n",
      "I1=2200  #Assuming losses\n"
     ],
     "language": "python",
     "metadata": {},
     "outputs": [
      {
       "output_type": "stream",
       "stream": "stdout",
       "text": [
        "N1xAc= 0.938438438438\n",
        "N1= 18 turns\n",
        "N2= 1800 turns\n",
        "x= 228.331926813 mm\n",
        "I2= 21.6666666667 A\n"
       ]
      }
     ],
     "prompt_number": 15
    },
    {
     "cell_type": "markdown",
     "metadata": {},
     "source": [
      "**Note that** :Primary winding current is higher than 21.67*100=2167 A due to magnetizing current and core loss modelling\n",
      " \n",
      " (I1 > 2167 A)\n",
      " \n",
      " Also we know that I1 is around 2167 A \n",
      " \n",
      " So assumme that I1=2200 A "
     ]
    },
    {
     "cell_type": "heading",
     "level": 3,
     "metadata": {},
     "source": [
      "**3) SELECTION OF PROPER COPPER CABLE**"
     ]
    },
    {
     "cell_type": "code",
     "collapsed": false,
     "input": [
      "# Assume that current carrying capabilty of cable is equal to 4 A / mm^2\n",
      "cur_carr_cap=4,\n",
      "# For primary winding\n",
      "Area1=2167.0/4.0\n",
      "Area2=21.67 /4.0\n",
      "print 'Area1=',Area1, 'mm^2'\n",
      "print 'Area2=',Area2, 'mm^2'\n",
      "\n",
      "\n"
     ],
     "language": "python",
     "metadata": {},
     "outputs": [
      {
       "output_type": "stream",
       "stream": "stdout",
       "text": [
        "Area1= 541.75 mm^2\n",
        "Area2= 5.4175 mm^2\n"
       ]
      }
     ],
     "prompt_number": 16
    },
    {
     "cell_type": "markdown",
     "metadata": {},
     "source": [
      "Therefore, \n",
      "\n",
      "**Total Conductor(Copper) Area of Primary Side > 541.75 mm^2 **\n",
      "\n",
      "**Total Conductor(Copper) Area of Secondary Side > 5.4175 mm^2**\n",
      "             "
     ]
    },
    {
     "cell_type": "code",
     "collapsed": false,
     "input": [
      "#Skin Depth Calculation for Copper cable at 500 Hz\n",
      "#p=1.68*10**-8 # Copper resistivity at 20 'C\n",
      "c=0.00386 # Temperature coefficient of copper per degree\n",
      "p=(1.68+ 90*c)*10**-8 # resistivity of copper at 110 'C\n",
      "f=500.0 # Hz\n",
      "w=2*pi*f\n",
      "u=4*pi*0.999991e-7\n",
      "Skin_Depth=sqrt((2*p) / (w*u))*1000 # in mm\n",
      "print 'Skin_Depth=',Skin_Depth,'mm'\n",
      "\n"
     ],
     "language": "python",
     "metadata": {},
     "outputs": [
      {
       "output_type": "stream",
       "stream": "stdout",
       "text": [
        "Skin_Depth= 3.20484333861 mm\n"
       ]
      }

      "Effective_Copper_Area_1=Total_Copper_Cable_Area_1-Non_Efffective_Copper_Area_1\n",

     "source": [
      "This transformer is used for HVDC transmission in order to step up voltage.For this purpose ,500 Hz AC transformer is designed.\n",
      "\n",
      "First of all, two different core materials are selected which have 0.35 mm thickness and 0.2 mm thickness.Core-1(0.35 mm thicknes core) has higher core loss in terms W/kg.Therefore, it has higher core loss since core dimensions are same for two different materials or laminations.In other words, Core Material-2 (0.2 thickness core) is more suitable for this power transformer due to efficiency criteria.\n",
      "\n",
      "Secondly, turn number and core area are calculated.This is important part because it shows that turn number and core dimensions are directly related each other and there is a inverse relationship between turn number and core area.\n",
      "\n",
      "Other important part is selection of proper copper cable for primary and secondary winding.Current carrying capacity (related to cooling), primary and secondary currents and skin depth are main parameters in order to determine proper cable because current carrying capability and primary and secondary currents specifiy required conductor area and skin depth specifies radius of cable.In addition, these parameters are used for other core are dimensions such as Window area,window length ,etc.  \n",
      "\n",
      "Another important issue is core loss and copper loss since they determine efficiency of transformer.In this desgin, core loss is much higher than copper loss.Actually, it is not desired desgin paramater.Generally, copper loss and core loss should be same as soon as possible in order to obtain high efficiency.For this purpose, turn number of coils can be increased to decrease core area or another material which has higher saturation flux density  can be used.However optimization is not considered in this project directly.\n",
      "\n",
      "After design is completed, output voltage at full load is 301 kV insted of 300 kV.The reason of this is phase shift due to leakge inductances.Note that for real transformer, there is tap changer to adjust suitable voltage for different load conditions.\n",
      "\n",
      "\n",
      "\n",
      "\n",
